<script>
    jQuery(function () {
        try {
            jQuery.support.placeholder = false;
            test = document.createElement('input');
            test2 = document.createElement('textarea');
            if ('placeholder' in test) jQuery.support.placeholder = true;
            if ('placeholder' in test2) jQuery.support.placeholder = true;
        } catch (e) { }
    });
    $(function () {
        try {
            if (!$.support.placeholder) {
                try {
                    var active = document.activeElement;
                    $('input, textarea').focus(function () {
                        if ($(this).attr('placeholder') != '' && $(this).val() == $(this).attr('placeholder')) {
                            $(this).val('').removeClass('hasPlaceholder');
                        }
                    }).blur(function () {
                        if (($(this).attr('placeholder') != '' && $(this).attr('placeholder') != undefined) && ($(this).val() == '' || $(this).val() == $(this).attr('placeholder'))) {
                            $(this).val($(this).attr('placeholder')).addClass('hasPlaceholder');
                        }
                    });
                    $('input, textarea').blur();
                    $(active).focus();
                    $('form').submit(function () {
                        $(this).find('.hasPlaceholder').each(function () { $(this).val(''); });
                    });
                } catch (e) { }
            }
        } catch (e) { }
    });
var parseJSON = $.parseJSON;
</script>

                <script>                    function fbs_click() {
                        u = document.URL; t = document.title;
                        window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(u) + '&t=' + encodeURIComponent(t),
                  'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=726,height=536'); return false;
                    }

                    $(".tweet").click(function(event) {
                        var width = 575,
                        height = 400,
                        left = ($(window).width() - width) / 2,
                        top = ($(window).height() - height) / 2,
                        url = this.href,
                        opts = 'status=1' +
                                 ',width=' + width +
                                 ',height=' + height +
                                 ',top=' + top +
                                 ',left=' + left;

                                        window.open(url, 'twitter', opts);

                                        return false;
                    });
                      
                      </script>

              <span class="NOTE_Body"><div class='scriptInclude'></div><p align="justify">Mientras la ciudad de Colonia trata de recuperarse de la cadena de robos y agresiones sexuales cometidas por refugiados la pasada Nochevieja, que se registraron unas 500 denuncias, de las cuales un 40% eran denuncias por agresi&oacute;n sexual.</p><BR><p align="justify">En la apertura del carnaval este jueves, vigilada por unos 2000 polic&iacute;as que intentaban garantizar la seguridad. M&aacute;s del doble de personal que hubo el a&ntilde;o pasado, debido a la petici&oacute;n de la alcaldesa de Colonia de reforzar la presencia policial y blindar la ciudad para que no se vuelva a repetir lo pasado en Nochevieja.</p><BR><p align="justify">Tan s&oacute;lo en el primer d&iacute;a de carnaval, las denuncias por agresiones han sido m&aacute;s del doble que el a&ntilde;o pasado, 22 en total.</p><BR><p align="justify">Dos de las agresiones han sido extremadamente graves. Una de las v&iacute;ctimas es una reportera de televisi&oacute;n belga. Esta periodista fue manoseada y agredida sexualmente con la c&aacute;mara en marcha.</p><BR><p align="justify">El segundo caso es el de una mujer que en la madrugada del viernes, de camino a casa, recibi&oacute; una paliza y fue violada.</p><BR><p align="justify">La Polic&iacute;a, que ha pedido la colaboraci&oacute;n ciudadana, analiza grabaciones de v&iacute;deo y mensajes de las redes sociales enviados por norteafricanos, as&iacute; como la presencia en Colonia de individuos llegados de fuera de Europa, as&iacute; como de pa&iacute;ses vecinos como B&eacute;lgica, Holanda y Francia.</p></span>

    nn=(document.layers)?true:false;
    ie=(document.all)?true:false;
    var lastKey;
    function keyDown(e) {
	    var evt=(e)?e:(window.event)?window.event:null;
	    if(evt){
		    var key=(evt.charCode)?evt.charCode:
			    ((evt.keyCode)?evt.keyCode:((evt.which)?evt.which:0));
		    lastKey = key;
	    }
    }
    document.onkeydown=keyDown;
    if(nn) document.captureEvents(Event.KEYDOWN);

    var qLookup = '';
    function LookUpUsers(obj)
    {
       
        if(GetTag('contentPublic'))
            {
                GetTag('contentPublic').style.display = 'none';
            }
        if(obj.value.length > 1 && obj.value != obj.placeholder)
        {   
            if(GetTag('globalUsersTable'))
            {
                GetTag('globalUsersTable').style.zIndex = -1;
            }
            qLookup = obj.value;
            $('.PublicityInLeft').fadeOut('fast');
            $("#lookup").fadeTo('fast', 1) ;
             $("#lookup").css('display', 'block') ;
            //GetTag('lookup').style.display = 'block';
            GetTag('lookup').innerHTML = '<div height="200" style="height:200px; width:100%" align="center"><br><br><br><img  src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/loading_spin.gif"></div>'
            
            //$.post('http://www.bouex.com/Content/ASP/Footer.asp', {IsAjax: "lookup", str: obj.value.replace(/ /gi, '_')}, drawLookup)
            doAjax('../../Content/ASP/Footer.asp', 'IsAjax=lookupJSON&str=' + obj.value.replace(/ /gi, '_'),'POST','', drawLookup);
        }else{
            //GetTag('lookup').innerHTML = '';
        }
    }

    function LogonSubmitForm() {
            if (GetTag('Login').value.length == 0 || GetTag('Password').value.length == 0) {
                GetTag('Login').focus();
                return false;
            }
            document.LogonHeader.LogonSubmit.value = 'LogonSubmit';
            document.LogonHeader.submit();
        }   
    function ExpandWSNews(idWS)
    {
        originNews(GetTag('WSNewsContentURL_' + idWS).value);
        return;
        GetTag('WSNewsExpanded').style.display = 'block';
         GetTag('WSNewsExpanded').style.color = 'black';
         GetTag('WSNewsExpanded').style.padding = "15px 15px 15px 15px";
         $("#WSNewsExpanded").animate({width: "38%",    opacity: 1,    marginLeft: "0.6in",    borderWidth: "3px", left:"25%"}, 1500 );
        GetTag("WSNewsExpandedContentSpan").innerHTML = '<div class="NOTE_Title" style="line-height:40px">' + GetTag('WSNewsTitle_' + idWS).value + '</div><br><br>' + GetTag('WSNewsContent_' + idWS).value + '<br><br><div style="text-align:right"><span class="linkImit" onclick="originNews(\'' + GetTag('WSNewsContentURL_' + idWS).value + '\')">+</a></div>';

    }
    function LookUpUsersBody(obj)
    {
        if(obj.value.length > 1)
        {
            GetTag('lookupBody').style.display = 'block';
            GetTag('lookupBody').innerHTML = '<div height="200" style="height:200px; width:200px" align="center"><br><br><br><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/loading_spin.gif"></div>'
            doAjax('http://www.bouex.com/Content/ASP/Footer.asp', 'IsAjax=lookup&str=' + obj.value,'POST','', drawLookupBody);
        }else{
            //GetTag('lookup').innerHTML = '';
        }
    }

    function originNews(urlWS)
    {
        $("#WSNewsExpanded").css("display", "none");
        $("#spinningImg").css("display", "block");
        
        $("#WSOriginURLfram").html("<iframe onload='closeSpinning()' style='border:0px; width:100%; height:95%' src='" + urlWS + "'>");
        $("#WSOriginURL").css("display", "block");
    }
    function closeSpinning()
    {
        $("#spinningImg").css("display", "none");
    }
	
    var drawLookup = function()
    {
        if (ajax.readyState == 4) {
             var ret = parseJSON(ajax.responseText);

             
             var ary = new Array();

             ary.push('<div class="linkImit" width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" align="right" onclick="GetTag(\'lookup\').style.display=\'none\'; ">X</div>');
            
             if(ajax.responseText.length==0)
             {
                GetTag('lookup').innerHTML = '<div align="center" style="font-size:11px;">No results found.</div>';
                return;
             }else{
             }

             var id;
             var name; 
             var isWhat;
             var img;
             var tLoginName;
             var shortName;
             for(i=0; i<ret.length; i++)
             {
                if(ret[i].length>0 || true)
                {
                    isWhat = ret[i].type;
                    id = ret[i].ID;
                    name = ret[i].name;
                    img = ret[i].image.replace('\\', '/').toLowerCase();
                    tLoginName = ret[i].login;
                    shortName = (ret[i].name.length > 30)?ret[i].name.substr(0,30) + '...':ret[i].name;
                    switch(isWhat)
                    {
                        case 'Login':
                            if(img.indexOf('.jpg') != -1)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table class="" cellspacing=0 width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '_' + name + '\'"><tr style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" ><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/ProfileImages/' + img + '"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left;border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED" class="lookupContent" align="left"> ' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                        case 'Profile':
                            if(img.indexOf('.jpg') != -1)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '_' + tLoginName + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent"><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/ProfileImages/' + img + '"></td><td style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED;vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'MainPage':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + 'news/' + tLoginName + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED"><img height="40" onerror="this.src=\'http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/mainpage.jpg\'" src="http://www.bouex.com/UserImages/' + Right('000000' + id,6) + '/th/logo.jpg"></td><td style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED;vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'Note':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + 'news/' + tLoginName + '/' + id + '_Note.htm\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent"><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/notepad.jpg"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'GlobalMainPage':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + name.replace(/ /gi, '') + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent" style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED"><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/global.png"></td><td style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED; vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'NewsKey':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" title="NewsKey" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '!' + name.replace(/ /gi, '') + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent" style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED"><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/open.png"></td><td style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED; vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> !' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                    }
                }
             }
              ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + 'Advanced?q=' + qLookup + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED; background-color:rgb(192, 232, 169); color:green" colspan=2 align=center> more results +  </td></tr>');
              ary.push('</table>');
             GetTag('lookup').innerHTML = ary.join('');
             }
    }

    var drawLookupBody = function()
    {
        if (ajax.readyState == 4) {
             var ret = ajax.responseText.split(String.fromCharCode(29));

             
             var ary = new Array();

             ary.push('<div class="linkImit" width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" align="right" onclick="GetTag(\'lookupBody\').style.display=\'none\'">X</div>');
            
             if(ajax.responseText.length==0)
             {
                GetTag('lookupBody').innerHTML = '<div align="center" style="font-size:11px;">No results found.</div>';
                return;
             }else{
             }

             var id;
             var name; 
             var isWhat;
             var img;
             var tLoginName;

             for(i=0; i<ret.length; i++)
             {
                if(ret[i].length>0)
                {
                    isWhat = ret[i].split("*:+")[2];
                    id = ret[i].split("*:+")[0];
                    name = ret[i].split("*:+")[1];
                    img = ret[i].split("*:+")[3].replace('\\', '/').toLowerCase();
                    tLoginName = ret[i].split("*:+")[4];

                    switch(isWhat)
                    {
                        case 'Login':
                            if(img.indexOf('.jpg') != -1)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table class="lookupContent" width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '_' + name + '\'"><tr ><td width="15" ><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/ProfileImages/' + img + '"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" class="lookupContent" align="left"> ' + name + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                        case 'Profile':
                            if(img.indexOf('.jpg') != -1)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '_' + tLoginName + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"><td width="15" class="lookupContent"><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/ProfileImages/' + img + '"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + name + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'MainPage':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + 'news/' + tLoginName + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"><td width="15" class="lookupContent"><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/mainpage.jpg"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + name + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'Note':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + 'news/' + tLoginName + '/' + id + '_Note.htm\'"><tr class="lookupContent"><td width="15" class="lookupContent"><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/notepad.jpg"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + name + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'GlobalMainPage':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + name.replace(/ /gi, '') + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"><td width="15" class="lookupContent"><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/global.png"></td><td style="vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> ' + name + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                         case 'NewsKey':
                            if(tLoginName.length>0)
                            {
                                ary.push('<table width="100%" cellspacing=0 style="cursor:pointer;" title="NewsKey" onclick="location.href = \'' + webPath + '!' + name.replace(/ /gi, '') + '\'"><tr class="lookupContent"  style="border-bottom:1px solid"><td width="60" class="lookupContent" style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED"><img height="40" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/open.png"></td><td style="border-bottom:1px solid #EDEDED; vertical-align:middle; text-align:left" align="left" class="lookupContent"> !' + shortName + '</td></tr>');
                                ary.push('</table>');
                            }
                            break;
                    }
                }
             }
             GetTag('lookupBody').innerHTML = ary.join('');
             }
    }

    function isDay()
    {
        var hr = (new Date()).getHours();
        var ret = (hr<7 || hr>19)?false:true;
        return ret; 
    }
    function loadWeather()
       {
           if(!isDay())return;

           $.ajax({ 
            data: {Remote_ADDR: '128.82.4.244', isDay:isDay()}, 
            type: "POST", 
            url: "../../Content/ASP/GetWeather.asp", 
            timeout: 20000, 
            contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=ISO-8859-15", 
            dataType: 'text', 
            success: function(data){

                $("#WeatherTDInline").html(data);
                 $("div.currentWeather").click(function() { 
                        $(".FutureWeather").toggle("200");
                    });

                    $(".FutureWeather").click(function(){
                        $(".FutureWeather").toggle("200");
                        });

                    try{
                        if(data.length==0)
                        {
                            loadWeatherUser();
                        }
                    }catch(e){}
                } 
        }); 
       }

    function GetHelp(by)
    {
        var screenHeight = $('body').innerHeight();
         GetTag('background').style.height = screenHeight + 'px';
         $("#background").css({ "opacity": "0.4" })
							.fadeIn("fast");
         $("#contentHelp").fadeIn("fast");
        
        switch(by)
        {
            case 'GlobalMainPage':
                GetTag('contentHelpcontent').innerHTML = 'On Register you have selected a Country and State. As you already know on boueX you are <b>FREE to PUBLISH</b> what you want when ever you want without restrictions and every news you post will be shown on your Newspaper WITHOUT LIMITS until you decide the opposite. <br>But you need to remember that every News Published has the chance to be part of the GLOBAL Newspaper of your State or Country, depending on the selection you made at the moment of Publishing this news. <br><br>i.e. if you are registered to California, United States, at the moment of Publish a new News you will have to choose where will this be connected to, to the California or to the Country GLOBAL Newspaper when this News  reaches the minimum Score required, and of course it depends on your decision that will depend on the content of this News. <br>But you must be wondering, what is needed to reach these Global Newspapers, the answer is very simple: All Active News Scored with over 20pts can be shown on a GLOBAL Newspaper. <br><br>You will get a confirmation email once a news of your own reach this page and a you will see a Mark to the left of every Titles that are ranked to be a GLOBAL News.';
                break;
        }
    }

    function isEmail(e)
    {
        var regex = /^[a-zA-Z0-9._-]+@([a-zA-Z0-9.-]+\.)+[a-zA-Z0-9.-]{2,4}$/;
        return regex.test(e);
    }
    function SendRecoveredPass()
    {
        var email_ = GetTag('emailRecover').value;
        if(email_.length == 0 || !isEmail(email_))
        {
            GetTag('emailRecover').style.border = '2px solid Red';
            return false;
        }else
        {
            GetTag('emailRecover').style.border = '1px solid #DFDFDF';
        }
        
        GetTag('RecoverPassDivContent').innerHTML = '<div align="center"><img height="30" src="http://www.bouex.com/Include/RootImages/loading_spin.gif"></div>'

        doAjax('http://www.bouex.com/Content/ASP/Footer.asp', 'body=We_sent_you_your_Password_so_you_can_Log_In_into_your_boueX_account_again._<br><br>Your_Password_is:_<b>{Password}</b><br>&subject=Your_Password_on_boueX!&IsAjax=RecoverPass&email=' + email_.replace(/ /gi, '+++'),'POST','', SendRecoveredPassCallBack);
    }

    var SendRecoveredPassCallBack = function()
    {
        if (ajax.readyState == 4) {
             var ret = ajax.responseText;
             
             switch(ret)
             {
                case '0':
                    GetTag('RecoverPassDivContent').innerHTML = '<br><div align="center">Your Password was sent to your Email address, check your inbox in a ew minutes and you will be able to Log In again to boueX!</div>';
                    GetTag('RecoverPassDivInput').style.display = 'none';
                    break;
                case '-1':
                    GetTag('RecoverPassDivContent').innerHTML = '<br><div align="center">There is not an Account linked to this Email Address.</div>';
                    break;
               default:
                    GetTag('RecoverPassDivContent').innerHTML = '<br><div align="center">There was an error processing your request. Please contact <span class="ErrorSupport()" class="linkImit">Technical Support</span></div>';
                    GetTag('RecoverPassDivInput').style.display = 'none';
                    break;
             }
         }
    }

     function toggleGroup(gid) {
       for (var i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
           if (i != gid) {
               $("#group" + i).slideUp("slow");
           }
        }
        $("#group" + gid).slideToggle("200");
    }

    function toggleLogin()
       {
        try{
           $("#toggleLoginDiv").center();
           }catch(e){}
           $("#toggleLoginDiv").css({"top":"100px"});
           $("#toggleLoginDiv").toggle("00");

           return;
            if(GetTag('toggleLoginDiv').style.left != '230px')
           {
                $("#toggleLoginDiv").css("display", "block");
                $("#toggleLoginDiv").animate({left: '230px'}, 300);
               
           }else
           {
               $("#toggleLoginDiv").animate({left: '-230px'}, 300);
               setTimeout('$("#toggleLoginDiv").css("display", "none");',200);
           }
       }
      
      var WOpacity = 1;
      function blinkWeather()
      {
        try{
            setInterval(function(){
                    $(".WheatherBar img").css({opacity:WOpacity})
                    if(WOpacity==1)
                    {
                        WOpacity = 0.95;
                    }else
                    {
                        WOpacity = 1;
                    }

                        var defaultVal = 'Search by Country, City, Title, Newspaper, Authors..';
                        $('#LookUpInput').focus(function () {
                            
                            if (this.value == defaultVal) {
                                this.value = '';
                            }
                            if (this.value != defaultVal) {
                                this.select();
                           
                            }
                             $(this).removeClass('hasPlaceholder');
                        });
                        $('#LookUpInput').blur(function () {
                            
                            if ($(this).val() == '') {
                                $(this).val( (defaultVal ? defaultVal : ''));
                                $(this).addClass('hasPlaceholder');
                            }

                        });
                        docHeight = $(document).height();
                        $(".backGralTable").css({height:docHeight});
                        
                    });

 jQuery.fn.center = function (bottom) {
                            this.css("position", "absolute");
                            if (bottom != undefined) {
                                this.css("bottom", bottom);
                            } else {
                                this.css("top", (($(window).height() - this.outerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop() - 75 + "px");
                            }
                            this.css("left", (($(window).width() - this.outerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft() + "px");
                            return this;
                        }
 // Used for trimming whitespace
	 try{
    trimLeft = /^\s+/,
	trimRight = /\s+$/,

	// Check for digits
	rdigit = /\d/,

	// Match a standalone tag
	rsingleTag = /^<(\w+)\s*\/?>(?:<\/\1>)?$/,
   
 jQuery.extend({
// A crude way of determining if an object is a window
	isWindow: function( obj ) {
		return obj && typeof obj === "object" && "setInterval" in obj;
	},
    isNaN: function( obj ) {
		return obj == null || !rdigit.test( obj ) || isNaN( obj );
	}

    
    });

 // Create innerHeight, innerWidth, outerHeight and outerWidth methods
jQuery.each([ "Height", "Width" ], function( i, name ) {

	var type = name.toLowerCase();

	// innerHeight and innerWidth
	jQuery.fn["inner" + name] = function() {
		return this[0] ?
			parseFloat( jQuery.css( this[0], type, "padding" ) ) :
			null;
	};

	// outerHeight and outerWidth
	jQuery.fn["outer" + name] = function( margin ) {
		return this[0] ?
			parseFloat( jQuery.css( this[0], type, margin ? "margin" : "border" ) ) :
			null;
	};

	jQuery.fn[ type ] = function( size ) {
		// Get window width or height
		var elem = this[0];
		if ( !elem ) {
			return size == null ? null : this;
		}

		if ( jQuery.isFunction( size ) ) {
			return this.each(function( i ) {
				var self = jQuery( this );
				self[ type ]( size.call( this, i, self[ type ]() ) );
			});
		}

		if ( jQuery.isWindow( elem ) ) {
			// Everyone else use document.documentElement or document.body depending on Quirks vs Standards mode
			// 3rd condition allows Nokia support, as it supports the docElem prop but not CSS1Compat
			var docElemProp = elem.document.documentElement[ "client" + name ];
			return elem.document.compatMode === "CSS1Compat" && docElemProp ||
				elem.document.body[ "client" + name ] || docElemProp;

		// Get document width or height
		} else if ( elem.nodeType === 9 ) {
			// Either scroll[Width/Height] or offset[Width/Height], whichever is greater
			return Math.max(
				elem.documentElement["client" + name],
				elem.body["scroll" + name], elem.documentElement["scroll" + name],
				elem.body["offset" + name], elem.documentElement["offset" + name]
			);

		// Get or set width or height on the element
		} else if ( size === undefined ) {
			var orig = jQuery.css( elem, type ),
				ret = parseFloat( orig );

			return jQuery.isNaN( ret ) ? orig : ret;

		// Set the width or height on the element (default to pixels if value is unitless)
		} else {
			return this.css( type, typeof size === "string" ? size : size + "px" );
		}
	};

});


}catch(e){}

        $(".MPLogo").height(75);
    }

     function ShowLogonComments() {
          var screenHeight = $('body').innerHeight();
         GetTag('background').style.height = screenHeight + 'px';

         if(GetTag("contentPublicComments").style.display == 'block')
         {
            $("#background").fadeOut("fast");
            $("#contentPublicComments").fadeOut("fast");

         {
            $("#background").css({ "opacity": "0.4" })
							.fadeIn("fast");

        }

     
     }

	            var w = $('#rating').css('width');
	            // eliminamos el px
	            var width_div = parseInt(w.slice(0, w.length - 2));

	            var valoracion_defecto_num = valoracion_defecto.toPrecision(2);
	            actualizarPos(valoracion_defecto, width_div);

	            $("#rating").mousemove(function (e) {

	                var x = e.pageX - this.offsetLeft;
	                $('#rating span.moving-bg').css('left', x);
	                $('#status2').html((Math.round(x * 100 / width_div / maxScore,2) > userScore) ? userScore : Math.round(x * 100 / width_div / maxScore,2));

	            });
	            $("#rating").click(function (e) {
	                // Obtenemos la posicion del cursor.
	                var x = e.pageX - this.offsetLeft;
	                // Obtenemos el resultado de la votacin
	                var r = Math.round(x * 100 / width_div / maxScore,2);


	                // Actualizamos el valor numerico
	                valoracion_defecto = (valoracion_defecto + r) / 2;
	                // lo mostramos en pantalla
	                //valoracion_defecto_num = valoracion_defecto.toPrecision(2);
	                //$('#status2').html(Math.round(valoracion_defecto_num,2));
                    valoracion_defecto_num = parseInt(GetTag('status2').innerHTML,10);
                   
                    ScoreNote(valoracion_defecto_num);
	                actualizarPos(valoracion_defecto, width_div);
	                // $('#msg').html("Has votado: " + r);
	            });

	            $("#rating").mouseout(function (e) {
	                $('#status2').html(Math.round(valoracion_defecto_num,2));
	                actualizarPos(valoracion_defecto, width_div);
	            });
                
                
	        }
            //loadRegistryScript();
	    });

<script>
    (function ($) {
        $.fn.getTextWidth = function () {
            var spanText = $("BODY #spanCalculateTextWidth");

            if (spanText.size() <= 0) {
                spanText = $("<span id='spanCalculateTextWidth' style='filter: alpha(0);'></span>");
                spanText.appendTo("BODY");
            }

            var valu = this.val();
            if (!valu) valu = this.text();

            spanText.text(valu);

            spanText.css({
                "fontSize": this.css('fontSize'),
                "fontWeight": this.css('fontWeight'),
                "fontFamily": this.css('fontFamily'),
                "position": "absolute",
                "top": 0,
                "opacity": 0,
                "left": -2000
            });

            return spanText.outerWidth() + parseInt(this.css('paddingLeft')) + 'px';
        };

        $.fn.getTextHeight = function (width) {
            var spanText = $("BODY #spanCalculateTextHeight");

            if (spanText.size() <= 0) {
                spanText = $("<span id='spanCalculateTextHeight' style='display:none'></span>");
                spanText.appendTo("BODY");
            }

            var valu = this.val();
            if (!valu) valu = this.text();

            spanText.text(valu);

            spanText.css({
                "fontSize": this.css('fontSize'),
                "fontWeight": this.css('fontWeight'),
                "fontFamily": this.css('fontFamily'),
                "top": 0,
                "left": -1 * parseInt(width) + 'px',
                "position": 'absolute',
                "display": "none",
                "width": width
            });

            return spanText.innerHeight() + 'px';
        };

        /** 
        * Adjust the font-size of the text so it fits the container. 
        * 
        * @param minSize     Minimum font size? 
        * @param maxSize     Maximum font size? 
        * @param truncate    Truncate text after sizing to make sure it fits? 
        */
        $.fn.autoTextSize = function (minSize, maxSize, maxHeight, truncate) {
            var _self = this,
        _width = _self.innerWidth(),
        _height = _self.innerHeight(),
        _textWidth = parseInt(_self.getTextWidth()),
        _textHeight = parseInt(_self.getTextHeight()),
        _fontSize = parseInt(_self.css('font-size'));

            while (_width - 30 > _textWidth) {
                if (minSize && _fontSize <= parseInt(minSize)) { $(".PublicHeader_Data").fadeIn("fast"); break; }
                if (maxHeight <= _textHeight) { $(".PublicHeader_Data").fadeIn("slow"); break; }
                _fontSize++;
                _self.css('font-size', _fontSize + 'px');

                _textWidth = parseInt(_self.getTextWidth());
                _textHeight = parseInt(_self.getTextHeight());
            }

            if (truncate) _self.autoTruncateText();
            $(".PublicHeader_Data").fadeIn("fast")
        };

        /** 
        * Function that truncates the text inside a container according to the 
        * width and height of that container. In other words, makes it fit by chopping 
        * off characters and adding '...'. 
        */
        $.fn.autoTruncateText = function () {
            var _self = this,
        _width = _self.outerWidth(),
        _textHeight = parseInt(_self.getTextHeight(_width)),
        _text = _self.text(),
        _truncated = false;

            // As long as the height of the text is higher than that 
            // of the container, we'll keep removing a character. 
            while (_textHeight > _self.outerHeight()) {
                _text = _text.slice(0, -1);
                _self.text(_text);
                _textHeight = parseInt(_self.getTextHeight(_width));
                _truncated = true;
            }

            // When we actually truncated the text, we'll remove the last 
            // 3 characters and replace it with '...'. 
            if (!_truncated) return;
            _text = _text.slice(0, -3);

            // Make sure there is no dot or space right in front of '...'. 
            var lastChar = _text[_text.length - 1];
            if (lastChar == ' ' || lastChar == '.') _text = _text.slice(0, -1);
            _self.text(_text + '...');
        };
    })(jQuery); 

</script>

      function ConfirmGetCredit() {
          $.ajax({
              type: "POST",
              url: '../../Content/ASP/LogonAjax.asp?IsAjax=ConfirmGetCredit&getCreditNewsKeyID=',
              async: true,
             
              success: callbackConfirm,
              error: function (a, b) { }
          });
      }
      function callbackConfirm(ret) {
          switch (parseInt(ret,10)) {
              case 101:
                  $("#regSimpleCallBackMsg").html('<b>You already applied to this NewsKey!</b>');
                  break;
              case 99:
                  $("#regSimpleCallBackMsg").html('<b>There was an errror processing your request, we are working on it. Try it back in a few minutes.</b>');
                  break;
              case 0:
                  $("#regSimpleCallBackMsg").html('<b>Your accreditation is in process. <br>You will get an email once the Editor accepts your application!</b>');
                  break; 
          }
      }

    $('#PasswordCommon').focus(
                function () {

                    $(this).replaceWith(pass);
                    pass.focus();

    var msgCallback = '';
    
    function LogonCommonSubmit() {
        if (document.LogonCommon.Login.value.length == 0 || document.LogonCommon.PasswordCommon.value.length == 0 || document.LogonCommon.Login.value == 'User' || document.LogonCommon.PasswordCommon.value == 'Password') {
            document.LogonCommon.Login.focus();
            return false;
        }
        try {
            var bodySend = ''
            var subjectSend = '';
            if(!GetTag('isAskingCredit').checked)
            {
                getCreditNewsKeyID = 0;
                getFollowNewsKeyID = 0;
                getFollowMainPageLoginName = '';
            }
            switch (true) {
                case getCreditNewsKeyID > 0:
                    msgCallback = 'Your accreditation is in process. <br>You will get an email once the Editor accepts your application!';
                    break;
                case getFollowNewsKeyID > 0:
                    msgCallback = 'Now you are Reader of this NewsKey!';
                    bodySend = '{userFollowing} is a new Reader of your NewsKey !{NewsKeyName}. <br>More you write, more Readers you will get.<br>Congratulations!<br>boueX.com';
                    subjectSend = '!{NewsKeyName}, a new Reader!';
                    break;
                case getFollowMainPageLoginName.length > 0:
                    msgCallback = 'You are already following this Newspaper!';
                    bodySend = '{ReaderName} is interested on what you Publish on your boueX Newspaper from now on, so he added you as a favorite Author!';
                    subjectSend = '{ReaderName} is your fan now!';
                    break;
            }
        } catch (e) { getCreditNewsKeyID = 0; getFollowNewsKeyID = 0;getFollowMainPageLoginName = ''; }
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '../../Content/ASP/LogonAjax.asp?IsAjax=LoginAjax&UserName=' + document.LogonCommon.Login.value + '&Password=' + document.LogonCommon.PasswordCommon.value + '&LogonSave=LogonSave&getCreditNewsKeyID=' + getCreditNewsKeyID + '&getFollowNewsKeyID=' + getFollowNewsKeyID + '&getFollowMainPageLoginName=' + getFollowMainPageLoginName + '&KeyName=&body=' + bodySend + '&subject=' + subjectSend,           
           
            success: callbackLogin
        }); 

       /* document.LogonCommon.LogonSubmit.value = 'LogonSubmit';
        document.LogonCommon.submit();*/
    }
    function callbackLogin(json) {
        try {
            json = $.parseJSON(json);
            if (json.login.LoginID > 0) {
                try{
                var inprocc_ = GetTag('isAskingCredit').checked;
                }catch(e){}
                if (inprocc_) {
                    $("#RegisterSimpleAjax_Main_Login").html('<br><b>' + msgCallback + '</b><br><br><div align=center style="width:100%; text-align:center"><input type="button" style="width:200px" value="Publish a News" class="FollowNewHeader" onclick="location.href=\'http://www.bouex.com/101/Publish_Start.htm\'" /></div>');
                } else {
                    $("#RegisterSimpleAjax_Main_Login").html('<br><div align=center style="width:100%; text-align:center"><input type="button" style="width:200px" value="Publish a News" class="FollowNewHeader" onclick="location.href=\'http://www.bouex.com/101/Publish_Start.htm\'" /></div>');
                }
            } else {
                $("#LogonCommonError").html('Your User or Password are invalids, please try it back.');
            }
        } catch (e) { }
    }

        }

        <script type="text/javascript">
            var inProcess = false;

            function CReg() {
                GetTag('SpinDiv').innerHTML = '<img src="../../Include/RootImages/ajax-loader.gif" border=0 />';

            function ReplaceCh(vl)
            {
                vl = vl.replace("\\", "");

                vl = vl.replace("ã", "a");
                vl = vl.replace("é", "e");
                vl = vl.replace("í", "i");
                vl = vl.replace("ú", "u");
                vl = vl.replace("ó", "o");
                vl = vl.replace("ñ", "n");
                vl = vl.replace("Ñ", "N");
                vl = vl.replace("'", "");
                vl = vl.replace("(", "");
                vl = vl.replace(")", "");
                vl = vl.replace(",", "");
                vl = vl.replace("à", "a");
                vl = vl.replace("Ã", "A");
                vl = vl.replace(/ /gi, "+++");
                return vl;
            }
            function SubmitUserData(by) {
                var Delim = String.fromCharCode(28);
                GetTag('RegDivMessageFinal').innerHTML = '';
                if (by == 'confirm') {
                    // GetTag('ConfirmReg').disabled = 'disabled';
                    if (!IsEmail('AddUser', 'Email')) {
                        alert('Email' + ' Is not valid.');
                        GetTag('Email').focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                    if (!inProcess) {
                        inProcess = true;

                        setTimeout('CReg()', 100);
                        var logoIconsrc = (GetTag('logoIcon').src.indexOf('default.jpg') != -1) ? '' : GetTag('logoIcon').src.replace('http://www.bouex.com/', '../../');

                        doAjax('../../Content/ASP/ConfirmRegAjax.asp', 'IsAjaxReg=1&getCreditNewsKeyID=' + getCreditNewsKeyID + '&SelectedLanguage=ENGLISH&captcha=' + GetTag('captchaText').value + '&data=' + ReplaceCh(GetTag('childdrop4d3345011206b').options[GetTag('childdrop4d3345011206b').selectedIndex].value) + Delim + ReplaceCh(GetTag('parentdrop1').options[GetTag('parentdrop1').selectedIndex].value) + "&email=" + GetTag('Email').value + '&IsAjax=Reg2&logoIcon=' + logoIconsrc, 'POST', '', ConfirmReg2);
                    }
                    return false;

                }
                
                try {


                    if (GetTag('RegisterLogin').value.length == 0 || GetTag('RegisterLogin').value == 'User') {
                        throw 'Login ' + ' is empty.';
                        GetTag('RegisterLogin').focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                    if (GetTag('NewPassword').value.length == 0 || GetTag('NewPassword').value == 'Password') {
                        throw 'Password' + ' is empty.';
                        GetTag('NewPassword').focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                   /* if (GetTag('NewPassword').value != GetTag('RPass').value) {
                        throw ' Passwords don\'t match.';
                        GetTag('NewPassword').focus();
                        return false;
                    }*/
                    if (GetTag('Name').value.length == 0 || GetTag('Name').value == 'Name') {
                        throw 'Name' + ' is empty.';
                        GetTag('Name').focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                    if (GetTag('LastName').value.length == 0 || GetTag('LastName').value == 'Last Name') {
                        throw 'Last Name' + ' is empty.';
                        GetTag('LastName').focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                  

                    CheckLogin(GetTag('RegisterLogin').value);

                    
                   
                } catch (e) {
                    alert(e);
                }
            }
            $('#NewPassword').focus(
                function () {
                    var pass = $('<input id="NewPassword" maxlength="30" class="textEntry" name="NewPassword" type="password">');
                    $(this).replaceWith(pass);
                    pass.focus();
                }
            ); 

            var ConfirmReg1 = function () {
                if (ajax.readyState == 4) {
                    var ret = ajax.responseText;
                    GetTag('RegTable').style.display = 'none';
                    GetTag('RegionTable').style.display = 'block';
                    GetTag('CaptchaTD').style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

            var ConfirmReg2 = function () {
                if (ajax.readyState == 4) {
                    var ret = parseInt(ajax.responseText, 10);
                    switch (ret) {
                        case 0:
                            GetTag('RegDiv').innerHTML = '';
                            GetTag('RegDivMessageFinal').innerHTML = 'Your register was successful!... In a few minutes you will receive a confirmation email containing a link that will activate your Account, click on this link and start to <b>Publish your News</b> right away! <br><b>*Note:</b>If you dont see the confirmation message on your inbox, check the junk mail folder just in case. If problem persist please contact <a href="#" onclick="GoSupport()">Technical Support</a>';
                            break;
                        case 102:
                            GetTag('RegTable').style.display = 'block';
                            GetTag('RegionTable').style.display = 'none';
                            GetTag('CaptchaTD').style.display = 'none';
                            GetTag('RegDivMessageFinal').innerHTML = '<font color="red"><b>This user is taken!</b></font>';
                            break;
                        case 108:
                            GetTag('RegTable').style.display = 'block';
                            GetTag('RegionTable').style.display = 'none';
                            GetTag('CaptchaTD').style.display = 'none';
                            GetTag('RegDivMessageFinal').innerHTML = '<font color="red"><b>The email address is associated to another account<br> To recover your Password <span class="linkImit" onclick="RecoverPassword()">click here</span></b></font>';
                            break;
                        case 99:
                            GetTag('RegDivMessageFinal').innerHTML = '<font color="red"><b>Wrong Captcha</b></font>';
                            break;

                    }

                    inProcess = false;
                    if(GetTag('SpinDiv'))GetTag('SpinDiv').innerHTML = '';
                }
            }

   <script>
       

       var sourceReg = $("#sourceRegister").html();
       $("#sourceRegister").html("")
       $("#targetRegister").append(sourceReg);

       setTimeout(function () {
           jQuery(function () {
               try {
                   jQuery.support.placeholder = false;
                   test = document.createElement('input');
                   test2 = document.createElement('textarea');
                   if ('placeholder' in test) jQuery.support.placeholder = true;
                   if ('placeholder' in test2) jQuery.support.placeholder = true;
               } catch (e) { }
           });
           $(function () {
               try {
                  
                       try {
                           var active = document.activeElement;
                           $('input, textarea').focus(function () {
                               if ($(this).attr('placeholder') != '' && $(this).val() == $(this).attr('placeholder')) {
                                   $(this).val('').removeClass('hasPlaceholder');
                               }
                           }).blur(function () {
                               if (($(this).attr('placeholder') != '' && $(this).attr('placeholder') != undefined) && ($(this).val() == '' || $(this).val() == $(this).attr('placeholder'))) {
                                   $(this).val($(this).attr('placeholder')).addClass('hasPlaceholder');
                               }
                           });
                           $('input, textarea').blur();
                           $(active).focus();
                           $('form').submit(function () {
                               $(this).find('.hasPlaceholder').each(function () { $(this).val(''); });
                           });
                       } catch (e) { }
                   
               } catch (e) { }
           });
       }, 1000);
   </script>
